    window.Bilbasen = window.Bilbasen || {};

    Bilbasen.LegacyReadyHandlers = (function (window, undefined) {

        var module = {},
            record = {
                readyHandlers: [],
                bindHandlers: []
            },
            ready = function (func) {
                record.readyHandlers.push(func);
            },
            custom = function (event, handler) {
                record.bindHandlers.push({
                    event: event,
                    handler: handler
                });
            };

        window.$ = function () {

            if (typeof arguments[0] === 'function') {
                record.readyHandlers.push(arguments[0]);
                return undefined;
            }

            if (arguments[0] === document) {
                return {
                    ready: ready,
                    bind: custom,
                    on: custom
                };
            }

            return undefined;
        };

        module.replay = function () {
            //window.console && window.console.table(record.readyHandlers);
            $.each(record.readyHandlers, function () {
                $(this);
            });

            //window.console && window.console.table(record.bindHandlers);
            $.each(record.bindHandlers, function () {
                $(document).on(this.event, this.handler);
            });
        };

        return module;
    }(window));
</script>
